                                    <script>
                                        function alxScanWinrate() {
                                            // minimal 92%
                                            const min = 92;
                                            const max = 99;
                                            const result = (Math.random() * (max - min) + min).toFixed(1);
                                            document.getElementById("alx-winrate").innerHTML = "WINRATE: <strong>" + result + "%</strong>";
                                        }
